	if = { 
		limit = {

			}

				tag = KIE

				name = "Fiodor"

	}

			limit = { 
				has_province_modifier = NO_ConsortOrigin
			}
			remove_province_modifier = NO_ConsortOrigin
		}

	if = { 
		limit = { 
			has_disaster = decentral_collapse_disaster
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					stability = -1
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				is_bankrupt = yes
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					legitimacy_equivalent = 50
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					prestige = 0
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					faction_influence = { 
						faction = FC_BU
						influence = 40
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					absolutism = 30
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				AND = { 
				}
			}
			every_subject_country = { 
				limit = {

					OR = { 
						is_subject = no

						is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
					}
				}
				TUR = { 
					num_of_cities = ROOT
					AND = { 
						OR = { 
							is_subject = no
							is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
							is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
						}
					}
					num_of_ports = 1
				}
			}
			country_event = { 
				id = flavor_cri.1
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = { 
					NOT = { 
						exists = TUR
					}
					AND = { 
						is_subject = yes
						NOT = { 
							is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
						}
						NOT = { 
							is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
						}
					}
					TUR = { 
						NOT = { 
							num_of_cities = ROOT
						}
					}
					TUR = { 
						AND = { 
							is_subject = yes
							NOT = { 
								is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
							}
							NOT = { 
								is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
							}
						}
					}
					TUR = { 
						NOT = { 
							num_of_ports = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			log = "FE-CRI:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:death_of_haji_giray flag set:on_regent"
		}
	}

on_weak_heir_claim = { 
	if = { 
		limit = { 
			NOT = { 
				AND = { 
					AND = { 
						has_reform = Pol_Succession5
						has_reform = Pol_Family3
					}
					has_reform = Pol_Tradition4
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = POP_Init
			NOT = { 
				AND = { 
					has_country_flag = Horde_Timur
					NOT = { 
						has_country_flag = Timur_Dead
					}
				}
			}
		}
		log = "FE:[GetYear]:[Root.GetName]:on ascension of heir with a weak claim, pretender spawned:on_weak_heir_claim"
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				AND = { 
					OR = { 
						AND = { 
							government = tribal
							OR = { 
								has_reform = Pol_Autonomy1
							}
							has_reform = Pol_Leadership1
							has_reform = Pol_Tradition4
						}
						AND = { 
							government = monarchy
							has_reform = Horde_MonarchyS
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_province = { 
				limit = { 
					is_capital = no
					is_overseas = no
					development = 3
				}
				pretender_rebels = 1
			}
			random_owned_province = { 
				limit = { 
					is_capital = no
					is_overseas = no
					development = 5
				}
				pretender_rebels = 2
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				num_of_cities = 5
				government = monarchy
			}
			random_owned_province = { 
				limit = { 
					any_neighbor_province = { 
						is_capital = yes
					}
				}
				pretender_rebels = 2
			}
		}
		else = { 
			random_owned_province = { 
				limit = { 
					is_capital = no
					is_overseas = no
					development = 5
				}
				pretender_rebels = 1
			}
		}
	}
	events = { }

on_adm_development = { 
	if = { 
		limit = { 
			base_tax = 0
		}
		add_base_tax = -1
	}
	if = { 
		limit = { 
			owner = { 
				ai = no
			}
		}
		owner = { 
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					OR = { 
						AND = { 
						}
						AND = { 
							NOT = { 
								has_country_flag = UI_Tooltip_On
							}
							AND = { 
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = { 
				limit = { 
					AND = { 
						is_wasteland = no
						NOT = { 
							province_id = 5154
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = Plague
			every_known_country = { 
				limit = { 
					AND = { 
						num_of_cities = 1
						NOT = { 
							tag = AAA
						}
					}
				}
				every_owned_province = { 
					limit = { 
						AND = { 
							is_wasteland = no
							NOT = { 
								province_id = 5154
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}
		add_mandate = -10
	}
}

					is_subject_of_type = personal_union_limited
				}
			}
			every_subject_country = { 
				limit = { 
					OR = { 
						is_subject_of_type = permanent_union
						is_subject_of_type = permanent_union_limited
					}
				}
				grant_independence = yes
				ROOT = { 
					create_subject = { 
						subject_type = permanent_union_limited
						subject = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
				break_marriage = PREV
				PREV = { 
					break_marriage = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	events = { }
}
on_dependency_lost = { 
	set_country_flag = tf_recalculate_communication_efficiency
	overlord = { 
		set_country_flag = tf_recalculate_communication_efficiency
	}
	FROM = { 
		set_country_flag = tf_recalculate_communication_efficiency
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { 
				AND = { 
					is_subject = yes
					NOT = { 
						is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
					}
					NOT = { 
						is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = tf_recalculate_communication_efficiency
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = { 
					is_subject_of_type = overseas_fief
					is_subject_of_type = personal_union
					is_subject_of_type = personal_union_limited
					is_subject_of_type = temporary_union
					is_subject_of_type = temporary_union_limited
					is_subject_of_type = permanent_union
					is_subject_of_type = permanent_union_limited
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				is_subject = yes
			}
			trigger_switch = { 
				on_trigger = is_subject_of_type
				vassal = { 
				}
				custom_vassal = { 
				}
				march = { 
				}
				client_vassal = { 
				}
				client_march = { 
				}
				colony = { 
				}
				protectorate = { 
				}
				tributary_state = { 
				}
				close_tributary_state = { 
				}
				appanage_subject = { 
				}
				daimyo_vassal = { 
				}
				decentralized_vassal = { 
				}
				rebellious_decentralized_vassal = { 
				}
				personal_union = { 
				}
				warlord = { 
				}
				overseas_fief = { 
				}
				temporary_union = { 
				}
				permanent_union = { 
				}
				muscovite_tributary_state = { 
				}
				commission = { 
				}
				personal_union_limited = { 
				}
				temporary_union_limited = {

on_capital_moved = { 
	log = "OnAction:[GetYear]:[Root.Owner.GetName]:changed capital from [From.GetName] to [This.GetName]:on_capital_moved"
	owner = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				is_part_of_hre = yes
				ROOT = { 
					is_part_of_hre = no
				}
			}
			set_in_empire = no
			swap_non_generic_missions = yes
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					hre_reform_passed = gemeinerpfennig
				}
				every_owned_province = { 
					limit = { 
						has_province_modifier = HRE_Gemeiner_Pfennig
					}
					remove_province_modifier = HRE_Gemeiner_Pfennig
				}
			}
			emperor = { 
				add_opinion = { 
					who = PREV
					modifier = hre_province_left
				}
			}
			add_imperial_influence = -1
			log = "OnAction:[GetYear]:[Root.Owner.GetName]:left HRE after moving its capital to [Root.GetName]:on_capital_moved"
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = tf_recalculate_communication_efficiency
			set_country_flag = AITax_Yearly
		}
		country_event = { 
			id = capital_city.001
		}
	}
	province_event = { 
		id = SYS_Colony.004
		days = 2
	}
}
